The child rubbed his hands and looked at his parents... We didn't know what happened when we got on the elevator... Let's talk about the food and beverage first. The buffet breakfast has very good Chinese dishes and many dishes. However, the Western dishes are a little bit worse. At the same time, for some reason, there are some useless interns standing in the buffet restaurant. They can neither help the employees clean up nor know what to ask. Basically, they are dull and have no basic awareness of food and beverage services. I don't know which hotel will unfortunately use them in the future.
Room facilities can be seen that they were carefully used in the past. Maybe it's a bit old. Some places, such as the floor, are a little worn. The highlight is that shampoo, lotion, etc. are still in small bottles. Australian essential oil brands are better than other five-star hotels.
The platform garden on the 3rd floor is definitely worth sitting. The view is very good. It's not high, but it's better because the Presidential Palace is opposite. There is no obstruction. The view from a distance is still good. I also saw two black swans. They are a little greedy and silly. They are very cute. It's a pleasant surprise.
Maybe because it's not a foreign-related hotel, there are few TV programs, only CCTV, which is relatively cheap. There's nothing to do.
In summary, it can be seen that this is a design concept with cultural heritage. The staff are generally friendly and enthusiastic, but the hotel management level is slightly poor. For example During the National Day holiday, around 2pm, there were many people checking in and out. There were only front desk staff, but no mobile positions to help the front desk, appease guests and understand in advance whether they were checking out or checking in, etc. Some guests who were checking out did not have to queue up, but because there was no hotel staff to help, they had to queue up and wait for the front desk. The pressure on the front desk was very high, including the incompetent problems of the cafeteria interns, which showed that the professional hotel management system needs to be improved. If the hotel wants to maintain a better operation, the management system needs to be improved. After all, the price is not cheap. It is a hotel with a good location and some expectations.
